Criteria_NNP to_TO qualify_VB for_IN hedge_JJ accounting_NN The_DT group_NN considers_VBZ its_PRP$ derivative_JJ financial_JJ instruments_NNS to_TO be_VB hedges_NNS when_WRB certain_JJ criteria_NNS are_VBP met_VBN ._.
